<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=strawberry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Strawberries_in_white_bowl.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Strawberries_in_white_bowl.jpg/220px-Strawberries_in_white_bowl.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Strawberries_in_white_bowl.jpg/330px-Strawberries_in_white_bowl.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Strawberries_in_white_bowl.jpg/440px-Strawberries_in_white_bowl.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1841" data-file-height="1381"></a><figcaption>Strawberries in a bowl</figcaption></figure>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=strawberry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/strawbery#Middle_English" title="strawbery">strawbery</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/strauberi#Middle_English" title="strauberi">strauberi</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/streawberge#Old_English" title="streawberge">strƒìawberƒ°e</a></i>, corresponding to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/straw#English" title="straw">straw</a></i> +‚Äé <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/berry#English" title="berry">berry</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=strawberry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Pronunciation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_English" class="extiw" title="w:British English">UK</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/Ààst…π…îÀêb(…ô)…πi/</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_English" class="extiw" title="w:American English">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/Ààst…π…îÀåb…õ…πi/</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cot%E2%80%93caught_merger" class="extiw" title="w:Cot‚Äìcaught merger"><i>cot</i>‚Äì<i>caught</i> merger</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/Ààst…π…ëÀåb…õ…πi/</span></li>
<li><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r50165410">.mw-parser-output .k-player .k-attribution{visibility:hidden}</style><table class="audiotable" style="vertical-align: middle; display:inline-block; list-style:none;line-height: 1em; border-collapse:collapse;"><tbody><tr><td class="unicode audiolink" style="padding-right:5px; padding-left: 0;">Audio (US, California)</td><td class="audiofile"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><span class="mw-tmh-player audio mw-file-element" style="width:175px;"><audio id="mwe_player_0_placeholder" preload="none" class="" width="175" style="width:175px;" data-durationhint="2" data-mwtitle="En-us-strawberry.ogg" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons" playsinline="" disabled="disabled" tabindex="-1"></audio><a class="mw-tmh-play" href="/wiki/File:En-us-strawberry.ogg" title="Play audio" role="button"><span class="mw-tmh-play-icon"></span></a><span class="mw-tmh-duration mw-tmh-label"><span class="sr-only">Duration: 2 seconds.</span><span aria-hidden="true">0:02</span></span></span></span></span></td><td class="audiometa" style="font-size: 80%;">(<a href="/wiki/File:En-us-strawberry.ogg" title="File:En-us-strawberry.ogg">file</a>)</td></tr></tbody></table></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=strawberry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">strawberry</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a> and <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/strawberries#English" title="strawberries">strawberries</a></b>)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>The sweet, usually <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/red#English" title="red">red</a>, edible <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/fruit#English" title="fruit">fruit</a> of certain plants of the genus <span class="biota"><a href="/wiki/Fragaria#Translingual" title="Fragaria"><i>Fragaria</i></a></span>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">They went to pick <b>strawberries</b> today.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Any plant of the genus <span class="biota"><a href="/wiki/Fragaria#Translingual" title="Fragaria"><i>Fragaria</i></a></span> (that bears such fruit).
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;‚ñº</a></span><dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">She has the best <b>strawberry</b> patch I've ever seen.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1886</b></span>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Peter_Christen_Asbj%C3%B8rnsen" class="extiw" title="w:Peter Christen Asbj√∏rnsen">Peter Christen Asbj√∏rnsen</a>, translated by H.L. Br√¶kstad, <cite>Folk and Fairy Tales</cite>, page <span class="None" lang="und">170</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">He told his father, and said it would be just suitable work for him to run about fields and woods amongst the <b>strawberry</b> hills after a flock of hares, and now and then lie down and take a nap on some sunny hill.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A dark <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/pinkish#English" title="pinkish">pinkish</a> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/red#English" title="red">red</a> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/color#English" title="color">colour</a>, like that of the fruit; <a href="/w/index.php?title=strawberry_red&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="strawberry red (page does not exist)">strawberry red</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel">strawberry: <span style="background-color:#B64140; display:inline-block; width:80px;">&nbsp;</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#rare" title="Appendix:Glossary">rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> Something resembling a strawberry, especially a reddish bruise, <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/birthmark#English" title="birthmark">birthmark</a>, or infantile <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/hemangioma#English" title="hemangioma">hemangioma</a> (<a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/naevus#English" title="naevus">naevus</a>).
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;‚ñº</a></span><dl><dd><span class="h-usage-example collocation"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/strawberry_mark#English" title="strawberry mark"><b>strawberry</b> marks</a></i></span></dd></dl>
<ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2024</b> February 20, Fiona Vera-Gray, quoting Almina, ‚Äú‚ÄòEverything is hairless‚Äô: what 100 women taught me about porn and body confidence‚Äù, in <cite>The Guardian</cite>‚Äé<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.theguardian.com/society/2024/feb/20/everything-is-hairless-what-100-women-taught-me-about-porn-and-body-confidence">[1]</a></sup>, <small><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/issn/0261-3077">‚ÜíISSN</a></small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">I have stretch marks and <b>strawberry</b> legs [follicles or blocked pores that appear as black dots]<sup style="font-style:normal">[<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#sic" title="Appendix:Glossary">sic</a></i>]</sup>; discoloration all over my body.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_English" class="extiw" title="w:American English">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> A <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/prostitute#English" title="prostitute">prostitute</a> who exchanges sexual services for <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/crack_cocaine#English" title="crack cocaine">crack cocaine</a>.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;‚ñº</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1987</b></span>, ‚ÄúDope Man‚Äù, in <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/N.W.A._and_the_Posse" class="extiw" title="w:N.W.A. and the Posse">N.W.A. and the Posse</a></cite>, performed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/N.W.A" class="extiw" title="w:N.W.A">N.W.A</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">Come home and see her mouth on the dopeman's dick / <b>Strawberry</b>, just look and you'll see her</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1992</b></span>, Kathleen Boyle, <cite>Homeless crack cocaine abusers</cite>, page <span class="None" lang="und">40</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en"><span class="q-hellip-sp"></span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>‚Ä¶<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> infamous in Los Angeles through media reports: the crack houses and "<b>strawberries</b>" (women who exchange sex for crack) <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>‚Ä¶<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></span></div></dd></dl></div></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=strawberry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Adjective"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">strawberry</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#comparative" title="Appendix:Glossary">comparative</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/strawberrier#English" title="strawberrier">strawberrier</a></b>, <i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#superlative" title="Appendix:Glossary">superlative</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/strawberriest#English" title="strawberriest">strawberriest</a></b>)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>Containing or having the flavor of strawberries.

<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>2011</b></span>, Hartley Pool, <cite>Stranger in Taiwan</cite>, Revenge Ink, <small><a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-0-9565119-6-6" title="Special:BookSources/978-0-9565119-6-6">‚ÜíISBN</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/strangerintaiwan0000pool/page/77/mode/1up">page <span class="None" lang="und">77</span></a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">Mind you, I have to admit they were three of the <b>strawberriest</b> looking strawberries I have ever seen.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>2013</b></span>, Caroline Green, <cite>Hold Your Breath</cite>, Piccadilly Press, <small><a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978_1_84812_170_6" title="Special:BookSources/978 1 84812 170 6">‚ÜíISBN</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/holdyourbreath0000gree_f7m2/page/125/mode/1up">page <span class="None" lang="und">125</span></a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">It was the <b>strawberriest</b> strawberry ever.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>2013</b></span> January, <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Front_(magazine)" class="extiw" title="w:Front (magazine)">Front</a></cite>, number <span class="None" lang="und">177</span>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/frontmagazine177/page/n37/mode/1up">page <span class="None" lang="und">38</span></a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">HANNAH SAYS: ‚ÄúWow, these are incredibly juicy. These are the <b>strawberriest</b> things in the world. They‚Äôre more strawberry[-]ish than actual strawberries. They‚Äôre incredible!‚Äù</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2022</b> June 9, Daniel Neman, ‚ÄúStrawberry spectacular‚Äù, in <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hartford_Courant" class="extiw" title="w:Hartford Courant">Hartford Courant</a></cite>, volume CLXXXVI, section 4, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/0ba-56888-3670-4f-77-8772-8cbbe-566d-890/page/n35/mode/1up">page 4</a>, column 1:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">Right now, strawberries are their <b>strawberriest</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Flavored with <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/ethyl_methylphenylglycidate#English" title="ethyl methylphenylglycidate">ethyl methylphenylglycidate</a>, an artificial compound which is said to resemble the taste of strawberries.</li>
<li>Of a colour similar to the colour of strawberry-flavoured products.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;‚ñº</a></span><dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The <b>strawberry</b> lipstick matched his outfit.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>2006</b></span>, Ida Liberkowski, Cynthia Malizia, <cite>Along the Amalfi Drive</cite>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lulu.com" class="extiw" title="w:Lulu.com">Lulu.com</a>, <small><a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/9781847285065" title="Special:BookSources/9781847285065">‚ÜíISBN</a></small>, page <span class="None" lang="und">282</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">They are, at once, beautiful and curious, with their translucent white skin and <b>strawberriest</b> blond hair, looking like a group of Wagner‚Äôs Valkyrie lost in a Puccini opera.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=strawberry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Verb"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">strawberry</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en s-verb-form-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/strawberries#English" title="strawberries">strawberries</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en ing-form-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/strawberrying#English" title="strawberrying">strawberrying</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en ed-form-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/strawberried#English" title="strawberried">strawberried</a></b>)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#intransitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">intransitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> To gather strawberries.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;‚ñº</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1994</b></span>, <cite>New England Review</cite>, volume <span class="None" lang="und">16</span>, page <span class="None" lang="und">35</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">We <b>strawberried</b> in Michigan woods with our fat nanny, and in spring we gathered sand dollars on Daytona, passed smiling into Kodachrome.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#intransitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">intransitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> To turn a dark pinkish-red.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;‚ñº</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1986</b></span>, Les Whitten, <cite>Sometimes a Hero</cite>, page <span class="None" lang="und">352</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">My hips and elbows were <b>strawberrying</b> painfully.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
